468. O*(O(C(//C(ClH)Cl)))
469. O*(C(//C(ClH)Cl))
470. C*(C(Cl//O)ClH)
471. O*(O(C(C(Cl//O)ClH)))
472. O*(C(C(Cl//O)ClH))
473. C(//C(ClH)//O)
474. C(C(ClHH)O(H)//O)
475. C(C(ClClH)ClO(H)H)
476. C(Cl#C(H))
477. C(ClC(HHH)//O)
478. C(//OC(HHH)O(H))
479. C(C(ClClH)ClClO(H))
The following is the reactino list
1. C(ClCl//C(ClH)) + O*(H) = C*(C(ClO(H)H)ClCl) [DA]
2. C(ClCl//C(ClH)) + Cl* = C*(C(ClClH)ClCl) [DA]
3. C(ClCl//C(ClH)) + O*(Cl) = C*(C(O(Cl)ClH)ClCl) [DA]
4. C(ClCl//C(ClH)) + Cl-*(Cl) = C*(C(ClClH)ClCl)+ Cl- [DA]
5. C*(C(ClO(H)H)ClCl) = C*(ClClC(//OH)) + HCl [XE]
6. C*(C(ClClH)ClCl) + O(//O) = O*(O(C(C(ClClH)ClCl))) [OA]
7. C*(C(O(Cl)ClH)ClCl) + O(//O) = O*(O(C(C(O(Cl)ClH)ClCl))) [OA]
8. C*(ClClC(//OH)) + O(//O) = O*(O(C(ClClC(//OH)))) [OA]
9. 2*O*(O(C(C(ClClH)ClCl))) = O*(C(C(ClClH)ClCl)) *2 + O2 [PB3]
10. 2*O*(O(C(C(ClClH)ClCl))) = O(C(C(ClClH)ClCl)O(C(C(ClClH)ClCl))) + O2 [PB4]
11. 2*O*(O(C(C(O(Cl)ClH)ClCl))) = O*(C(C(O(Cl)ClH)ClCl)) *2 + O2 [PB3]
12. 2*O*(O(C(C(O(Cl)ClH)ClCl))) = O(C(C(O(Cl)ClH)ClCl)O(C(C(O(Cl)ClH)ClCl))) + O2 [PB4]
13. 2*O*(O(C(ClClC(//OH)))) = O*(C(ClClC(//OH))) *2 + O2 [PB3]
14. 2*O*(O(C(ClClC(//OH)))) = O(C(ClClC(//OH))O(C(ClClC(//OH)))) + O2 [PB4]
15. C(ClCl//O) + H2O = CO2 + 2HCl [S]
16. O*(C(C(ClClH)ClCl)) = C(ClCl//O) + C*(ClClH) [BS]
17. O*(C(C(ClClH)ClCl)) = C(ClClHC(Cl//O)) + Cl* [BS]
18. O(C(C(ClClH)ClCl)O(C(C(ClClH)ClCl))) + O*(H) = C*(C(O(O(C(C(ClClH)ClCl)))ClCl)ClCl) + O(HH) [HA]
19. O(C(C(ClClH)ClCl)O(C(C(ClClH)ClCl))) + C*(C(ClClH)ClCl) = C*(C(O(O(C(C(ClClH)ClCl)))ClCl)ClCl) + C(ClClHC(ClClH)) [HA]
20. O(C(C(ClClH)ClCl)O(C(C(ClClH)ClCl))) + C*(C(O(Cl)ClH)ClCl) = C*(C(O(O(C(C(ClClH)ClCl)))ClCl)ClCl) + C(C(ClClH)O(Cl)ClH) [HA]
21. O(C(C(ClClH)ClCl)O(C(C(ClClH)ClCl))) + C*(ClClC(//OH)) = C*(C(O(O(C(C(ClClH)ClCl)))ClCl)ClCl) + C(ClClHC(//OH)) [HA]
22. O(C(C(ClClH)ClCl)O(C(C(ClClH)ClCl))) + Cl* = C*(C(O(O(C(C(ClClH)ClCl)))ClCl)ClCl) + Cl(H) [HA]
23. O(C(C(ClClH)ClCl)O(C(C(ClClH)ClCl))) + O*(Cl) = C*(C(O(O(C(C(ClClH)ClCl)))ClCl)ClCl) + O(ClH) [HA]
24. O(C(C(ClClH)ClCl)O(C(C(ClClH)ClCl))) + Cl-*(Cl) = C*(C(O(O(C(C(ClClH)ClCl)))ClCl)ClCl) + Cl- + Cl(H) [HA]
25. O*(C(C(O(Cl)ClH)ClCl)) = C(ClCl//O) + C*(O(Cl)ClH) [BS]
26. O*(C(C(O(Cl)ClH)ClCl)) = C(C(Cl//O)O(Cl)ClH) + Cl* [BS]
27. O(C(C(O(Cl)ClH)ClCl)O(C(C(O(Cl)ClH)ClCl))) + O*(H) = C*(C(O(O(C(C(O(Cl)ClH)ClCl)))ClCl)O(Cl)Cl) + O(HH) [HA]
28. O(C(C(O(Cl)ClH)ClCl)O(C(C(O(Cl)ClH)ClCl))) + C*(C(ClClH)ClCl) = C*(C(O(O(C(C(O(Cl)ClH)ClCl)))ClCl)O(Cl)Cl) + C(ClClHC(ClClH)) [HA]
29. O(C(C(O(Cl)ClH)ClCl)O(C(C(O(Cl)ClH)ClCl))) + C*(C(O(Cl)ClH)ClCl) = C*(C(O(O(C(C(O(Cl)ClH)ClCl)))ClCl)O(Cl)Cl) + C(C(ClClH)O(Cl)ClH) [HA]
30. O(C(C(O(Cl)ClH)ClCl)O(C(C(O(Cl)ClH)ClCl))) + C*(ClClC(//OH)) = C*(C(O(O(C(C(O(Cl)ClH)ClCl)))ClCl)O(Cl)Cl) + C(ClClHC(//OH)) [HA]
31. O(C(C(O(Cl)ClH)ClCl)O(C(C(O(Cl)ClH)ClCl))) + Cl* = C*(C(O(O(C(C(O(Cl)ClH)ClCl)))ClCl)O(Cl)Cl) + Cl(H) [HA]
32. O(C(C(O(Cl)ClH)ClCl)O(C(C(O(Cl)ClH)ClCl))) + O*(Cl) = C*(C(O(O(C(C(O(Cl)ClH)ClCl)))ClCl)O(Cl)Cl) + O(ClH) [HA]
33. O(C(C(O(Cl)ClH)ClCl)O(C(C(O(Cl)ClH)ClCl))) + Cl-*(Cl) = C*(C(O(O(C(C(O(Cl)ClH)ClCl)))ClCl)O(Cl)Cl) + Cl- + Cl(H) [HA]
34. O*(C(ClClC(//OH))) = C(Cl//OC(//OH)) + Cl* [BS]
35. O*(C(ClClC(//OH))) = C(ClCl//O) + C*(//OH) [BS]
36. O(C(ClClC(//OH))O(C(ClClC(//OH)))) + H2O = O(C(C(O(H)O(H)H)ClCl)O(C(ClClC(//OH)))) [HC]
37. C*(ClClH) + Cl* = C(ClClClH) [XR]
38. C*(ClClH) + Cl-*(Cl) = C(ClClClH) +Cl- [XR]
39. C*(ClClH) + O(//O) = O*(O(C(ClClH))) [OA]
40. C(ClClHC(Cl//O)) + H2O = C(C(ClClH)O(H)//O) + HCl [HX]
41. C*(C(O(O(C(C(ClClH)ClCl)))ClCl)ClCl) + O(//O) = O*(O(C(C(O(O(C(C(ClClH)ClCl)))ClCl)ClCl))) [OA]
42. C(ClClHC(ClClH)) + O*(H) = C*(C(ClClH)ClCl) + O(HH) [HA]
43. C(ClClHC(ClClH)) + C*(C(O(Cl)ClH)ClCl) = C*(C(ClClH)ClCl) + C(C(ClClH)O(Cl)ClH) [HA]
44. C(ClClHC(ClClH)) + C*(ClClC(//OH)) = C*(C(ClClH)ClCl) + C(ClClHC(//OH)) [HA]
45. C(ClClHC(ClClH)) + C*(ClClH) = C*(C(ClClH)ClCl) + C(ClClHH) [HA]
